------------------------------------------------------------------------
r1686 | t-anders | 2009-02-16 13:28:37 +0000 (Mon, 16 Feb 2009) | 2 lines
Changed paths:
   M /trunk/strasheela/source/MidiOutput.oz

Note off timing revised: when a note on event and the preceeding note off event occur at exactly the same time, some MIDI devices have problems. So far, Strasheela be default simply removed (OutputMidiFile arg removeQuestionableNoteoffs defaulted to true). Now, by default such note offs are very slightly moved forward (NoteToMidi new arg noteOffOffset defaults to ~0.003, measured in secs -- NoteToMidi is used by default for outputting MIDI notes (matching OutputMidiFile clause with test isNote).
